void quickSort(int* arr, int firstPos, int lastPos) { ^KcMLLAF2

// 1. Base Case: If the range has 0 or 1 element, it's already sorted. ^sw1F3rLB

if (firstPos >= lastPos) { ^ROynYveC

return; ^vt1FpfsV

} ^BSkpWhG4

// --- Partitioning Logic (Lomuto Scheme) --- ^YVYluazF

// We choose the last element as the pivot ^9OpF5KLA

int pivotValue = arr[lastPos]; ^vRsErXCW

// 'pointA' tracks the tail of the "smaller than pivot" section ^v9TvV1LE

int pointA = firstPos - 1; ^7FuGvvZE

for (int trav = firstPos; trav < lastPos; trav++) { ^uT4XHd0N

// If current element is smaller than or equal to pivot ^QKw69Tf4

if (arr[trav] <= pivotValue) { ^FEfiIOmQ

pointA++; ^qx97GrKZ

// Swap current element to the "smaller" section ^tWlme2uD

int temp = arr[pointA]; ^YIYuFNT6

arr[pointA] = arr[trav]; ^ctDN78mg

arr[trav] = temp; ^vE43mzuQ

} ^9hDVWOAQ

} ^JwhIz1a8

// Place the pivot in its correct sorted position ^YvGgZimA

// (Right after the last smaller element) ^tk3AzfsH

int partitionIndex = pointA + 1; ^jUxbcM5u

int temp = arr[partitionIndex]; ^NNrheGDC

arr[partitionIndex] = arr[lastPos]; ^o2myvdIk

arr[lastPos] = temp; ^tmE48b5C

// ------------------------------------------- ^IZOi1Xty

// 2. Recursive Calls ^IVadoFrn

// Sort the Left Subarray (elements smaller than pivot) ^KOz9cbhQ

quickSort(arr, firstPos, partitionIndex - 1); ^myb8Q70a

// Sort the Right Subarray (elements larger than pivot) ^xJsndP8I

quickSort(arr, partitionIndex + 1, lastPos); ^Y6YZaMVI

} ^S93uxJhw
